<script type='text/javascript'>
		//Start get param
		function getParameterByName(name){
		var errorCase='0';
		try{
		name = name.replace(/[\[]/, '\[').replace(/[\]]/, '\]');
		var regex = new RegExp('[\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)'),results = regex.exec(location.search);
		return results === null ? '' : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
		}
		catch(e){
		return errorCase;
		}
		}

		//End get param
		function readCookievideo(name) {
		var nameEQ = name + '=';
		var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
		for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
			var c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
			if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
		}
		return null;
		}
		var adRefferer = document.referrer;
		pageRefferer = '';
		if(adRefferer.indexOf('facebook.com') >= 0 ){
			pageRefferer ='facebook';
		}else if(adRefferer.indexOf('t.co') >= 0 ){
			pageRefferer ='twitter';
		}else if(adRefferer.indexOf('google.co.in') >= 0 ){
			pageRefferer ='google_search';
		}else if(adRefferer.indexOf('taboola') >= 0 ){
			pageRefferer ='taboola';
		}else if(adRefferer.indexOf('bhaskar') >= 0 ){
			pageRefferer ='bhaskar';	
		}
		</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
		function setTargetRepeat(){
			var timeDelay=189;
			var timeArray=[];
		//localStorage.clear('userTimeOut');
			if(typeof(Storage) !== 'undefined'){
				if(localStorage.getItem('userTimeOut')==null) {
					timeArray.push(new Date());
				try{
					localStorage.setItem('userTimeOut','timeArray');
					pubads.setTargeting('source','organic');
				}catch(e){
					pubads.setTargeting('source','organic');
				}
				}else {
					timeArray=(localStorage.getItem('userTimeOut').split(','));
					timeArray.push(new Date());
					try{
						localStorage.setItem('userTimeOut',timeArray);	
						if(diff()<=timeDelay && timeArray.length>=1 && pageRefferer!= ''){
							pubads.setTargeting('source','repeat');
						}else if(diff()<=timeDelay && timeArray.length==1 && pageRefferer == ''){
							pubads.setTargeting('source','organic');
						}else if(diff()>timeDelay  && pageRefferer == ''){
							timeArray=[];
							pubads.setTargeting('source','organic');
							localStorage.setItem('userTimeOut',timeArray);
							timeArray.push(new Date());
							localStorage.setItem('userTimeOut',timeArray);	
						}else{
							pubads.setTargeting('source','repeat');
						}
					}catch(e){
						pubads.setTargeting('source','repeat');
					}
				}
			}	
		
		function diff(){
			timeArray=(localStorage.getItem('userTimeOut').split(','));
			var t1=new Date(timeArray[0]);
			var t2=new Date(timeArray[timeArray.length-1]);
			var d=(t2-t1)/1000/60/60;
			return d;
		}
		}
		</script>

	var isOpen = false;
	submitButton.click(function(){
		if(isOpen == false){
		searchBox.addClass('searchOpen');
		isOpen = true;
		 }else{
		   searchBox.removeClass('searchOpen');
		   inputBox.focusout();
		   isOpen = false;
			}
		});

		submitButton.mouseup(function(){return false;});
		searchBox.mouseup(function(){return false;});
		$(document).mouseup(function(){
		   if(isOpen == true){ 
			$('.searchBtn').css('display','block');
			submitButton.click();
		  }
	});
function buttonUp(){
	var inputVal = $('.searchInput').val();
	inputVal = $.trim(inputVal).length;
		if(inputVal != 0){
			$('.searchBtn').css('display','none');
				}else{
				$('.searchInput').val('');
				$('.searchBtn').css('display','block');
				}
}
$(document).ready(function(){
	 
var today = new Date();
var dd = today.getDate();
var mm = today.getMonth()+1; //January is 0!
var yyyy = today.getFullYear();

if(dd<10){dd='0'+dd} if(mm<10){mm='0'+mm} today = dd+mm+yyyy;
	
	var readRfalSign = readCookie4Rashifal("rfalsign");
	if(readRfalSign)
	{
	 $("#rashifal-sticky-header").attr('href','http://religion.bhaskar.com/jyotish/rashifal/'+readRfalSign+'/today/'+today+'/');
	}
	 
 });
</script>

        source: function (request, response) {
			var term = $.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex(request.term)
                , startsWithMatcher = new RegExp("^" + term, "i")
                , startsWith = $.grep(source, function(value) {
                    return startsWithMatcher.test(value.label || value.value || value);
                })
                , containsMatcher = new RegExp(term, "i")
                , contains = $.grep(source, function (value) {
                    return $.inArray(value, startsWith) < 0 && 
                        containsMatcher.test(value.label || value.value || value);
                });
            response(startsWith.concat(contains));
        },

<script type='text/javascript'>
var pusherObj=$("#div-gpt-ad-1379583365650-0_ad_container").html();
if(typeof pusherObj == undefined || pusherObj == null){
	var elementOffset = $('.mBlue').offset().top;
		$(window).scroll(function(){
			var e = $(window).scrollTop();			
			var distance=(elementOffset-e);		  
		 if (e>=elementOffset){
			$(".mBlue").addClass("fixed")
			$(".hpicon a").removeClass("home-inner").addClass('gridIcon')
			 $('.hpicon a').attr({title: "Menu", href:"javascript:void(0)"});
			 $('.mNav li.home').addClass('inner_grid')
			}else{
				$(".mBlue").removeClass("fixed")
				$(".hpicon a").removeClass("gridIcon").addClass('home-inner')
				$('.hpicon a').attr({title: "होम", href:"http://www.bhaskar.com"});
				$('.stickyhover').hide()
				$('.mNav li').removeClass('nHover')
				$('.mNav li.home').removeClass('inner_grid')
				hover=false;
		  }
	});
}
var hover=false;
$('.mNav li:first-child').on('click',function(event){ 
event.stopPropagation();
	$('.stickyhover').slideToggle()
	$( this ).toggleClass( "nHover" );
});
$('.stickyhover').click(function(event){
event.stopPropagation();
});

$('.home').removeClass('nHover')
	});

	function loadvideo(id,autoplay){
		
		var shURL 		= 	'  /ajaxloadedition/'+id+'/';
		if(autoplay==0){
			$("#edition-container").html('');
		}
		else{
			$.ajax({ 
				type: "GET",
				data:{"autoplay":autoplay,'storyid':styid},
				url: shURL,
				success: function(data1) { 				
					$("#edition-container").html(data1);					
				},
				error: function(error) {
					//alert(error);
				}
			});
		}
	}


function getTrackFunction(tevent,vid_det,expand){
	
	$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		url:    '/non-cached/expand-colapse-track/',
		//dataType:"json",
		data: {'tevent':tevent,'vid_det':vid_det,'expand':expand},
		success: function (data){
		}
	 });
}

function readCookieBulletine(name) {
	var nameEQ = name + "=";
	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
		if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
	}
	return null;
	}
function createCookieBulletine(name,value,days) {
	if (days) {
		var date = new Date();
		date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
		var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
	}
	else var expires = "";
	var full = window.location.host
    var parts = full.split('.');
    var sub = parts[0];
    var domain = parts[1];
    var type = parts[2];
	if(type=='co'){
		type = type + '.' + parts[3];  	
	}
    var newDomain =  '.'+ domain + '.' + type;
	document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/;domain="+newDomain;
}
function getcurtimeajax(){
	 $.ajax({
			url:"/1-15-cached/getcurtime/1/", 
			type:'GET',			
			success: function(response){
				var thisUTStamp = new Date(response*1000);
				var hours = thisUTStamp.getHours();
				var minutes = thisUTStamp.getMinutes();
				//console.log(thisUTStamp +'=='+ hours + '==' + minutes );
				//console.log( hours + '>=12 && ' + hours +'<=13  || ' + hours +'>=19 &&'+ hours +'<=21' );
				
				if((readCookieBulletine('accordion_track') == null || readCookieBulletine('accordion_track') == 'null')){
					if((hours >= 7 && hours < 10) || (hours >= 18 && hours < 20 )){
						//----do nothing
					}else{																		
						//$('.accordion-toggle').click();		
						
					}
					
		   		}
			},
			
	});	
}

<script>
		
			var ct=1;
			var bid1=0;
			var flag1=0;
			var is_bolly=$("#is_bolly").val();
			var is_previous_bolly=$("#is_previous_bolly").val();
			$(".ja_pre_vid").click(function(e){
				
				
				if ($('#current_video').length==0 || flag1==1){
					return false;
				}
				flag1=1;
				if(ct%2!=0){
					var image_change = $("#thumburl_current").val();
					var ja_image_logo = $("#curr_bull_logo").val();
					bid1 = $("#bulletin_prev").val();
					changeText("prev_bull_label");
					changeClass();
					$(".janiye-time").text($("#bulletin_prev_time").val());
					
				
				}
				else{
					
					var image_change = $("#thumburl_prev").val();
					var ja_image_logo = $("#prev_bull_logo").val();
					bid1 = $("#bulletin_current").val();
					changeText("curr_bull_label");
					changeClass();
					$(".janiye-time").text($("#bulletin_current_time").val());
					
				}
				
				ct++;
				
				animate_next_vid();
				
				//document.getElementById('current_video').setAttribute('src', iframe_change);
				loadvideo(bid1,1);
				$("#pre_vid_image").attr("src",image_change);
				$("#left_vid_logo").attr("src",ja_image_logo);
				
			 });
			 
			function animate_next_vid(){
				var cart = $('#current_video');
				var imgtodrag =$("#pre_vid_image");
				
				
				if (imgtodrag) {
					var imgclone = imgtodrag.clone()
						.offset({
						top: imgtodrag.offset().top,
						left: imgtodrag.offset().left
					})
						.css({
						'opacity': '0.5',
							'position': 'absolute',
							'height': '150px',
							'width': '150px',
							'z-index': '100'
					})
						.appendTo($('body'))
						.animate({
						'top': cart.offset().top + 10,
							'left': cart.offset().left + 10,
							'width': 75,
							'height': 75
					}, 1000, 'easeInOutExpo');
					
					setTimeout(function () {
						cart.effect("", {
							times:0
						}, 200);
					}, 1500);

					imgclone.animate({
						'width': 0,
							'height': 0
					}, function () {
						$(this).detach()
					});
				}
			
			}

			function changeText(id){
				
				var $el = $('#agala_news');
				text = $("#"+id).val();
			
				$el.text(text);
				
				
				speed = 70; //ms

				$el.empty();

				var wordArray = text.split(' '),
					i = 0;
					
				
					INV = setInterval(function () {
						if (i >= wordArray.length - 1) {
							clearInterval(INV);
							flag1=0;
						}
						
							
							$el.append(wordArray[i] + ' ');
							i++;

					}, speed);
				
			
			}
			function changeClass(){
				
				if(is_bolly==1 || is_previous_bolly==1){
					$(".bulletin-content-bdr").toggleClass( "bulletin-content-bdr-bolly" );
					$(".bulletin-content").toggleClass( "bulletin-content-bolly" );
					$(".n_vid").toggleClass( "bolly_logo" );
					$(".jaab_logo,agala_news").fadeOut(550, function(){
						$(".bulletin-container").toggleClass( "bulletin-container-bolly" );
						$(".jaab_logo").fadeIn(1000);             
						$(".agala_news").fadeIn(1000);
					});  
				
					
					if($(".bulletin-content").hasClass( "bulletin-content-bolly" )){
						$("#accordion-track2").attr("title", "बॉलीवुड अभी ");
						$("#accordion-track1").attr("title", "बॉलीवुड अभी ");
						$(".ja_pre_vid").attr("title", " जानिए अभी");
						
					}
					else{
						$("#accordion-track2").attr("title", " जानिए अभी ");
						$("#accordion-track1").attr("title", " जानिए अभी ");
						$(".ja_pre_vid").attr("title", "बॉलीवुड अभी ");
					}
					
					
				}
				
			}
			function resetStripData(){
				
				if(ct>1){
					loadvideo(bid1,1);
				}
				
				
			}
		
			
			
			
				
	</script>

if(cityHomeEodGeoIPFirst=="" || typeof(cityHomeEodGeoIPFirst) == 'undefined'){
	var eodURL = "/non-cached/city-home-eod/";
	getEodData(eodURL,1);

	var eodURL = "/city-home-eod/"+cityHomeEodGeoIPFirst+"/";

	showTOPMessage(cityHomeEodGeoIPFirstchk);
}
function showTOPMessage(id){
		//$("#withoutajax").css({'display':'block !important'});
		$("#withoutajax").show();
		var mess = "";
		if(id=='uttar-pradesh'){
			mess = "यूपी";	
		}else if(id=='bhopal'){
			mess = "भोपाल";	
		}else if(id=='jaipur'){
			mess = "जयपुर";	
		}
		if(mess ==""){ return false;}
		
		var html = '<div id="city_eod_strip" class="cityEodStrip">आप पढ़ रहे हैं रेगुलर होम पेज, '+mess+' के लिए कस्टमाइज़्ड होमपेज पढ़ने के लिए <a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="getDefault2(1);">क्लिक करें</a>...<span onclick="getDefault2(2);" class="close">&nbsp;</span></div>';
		$("#bhaskar_eod").prepend(html);
		$( "#bhaskar_eod" ).find("h3").css({"font-size":"26px","line-height":"130%"});	
}
function getDefault2(type){
	if(type==2){
		$("#city_eod_strip").remove(); 
		$( "#bhaskar_eod" ).find("h3").css({"font-size":"30px","line-height":"130%"});	
	}else if(type==1){
		var cityHomeEodGeoIPFirstchk 	= getCookie('cityHomeEodGeoIPFirstchk');
		setCookie('cityHomeEodGeoIPFirstchk',100,10);
		setCookie('cityHomeEodGeoIPFirst',cityHomeEodGeoIPFirstchk,10);
		var eodURL = "/city-home-eod/"+cityHomeEodGeoIPFirstchk+"/";
		getEodData(eodURL,2);
	}
}
function getDefault(type){
	if(type==2){
		$( "#bhaskar_eod_new" ).find("h3").attr('style',$( "#bhaskar_eod" ).find("h3").attr('style'));
		$("#city_eod_strip").remove();
	}else{
		//$("#bhaskar_eod").show();
		jQuery("#withoutajax").show();
		//$("#withoutajax").css({'display':'block !important'});
		//$("#bhaskar_eod_new").hide();
		$("#firstEodNews").removeClass("up_news");
		$("#city_eod_strip").remove();
		$("#bhaskar_eod_new").hide();
		var cityHomeEodGeoIPFirst 	= getCookie('cityHomeEodGeoIPFirst');
		setCookie('cityHomeEodGeoIPFirstchk',cityHomeEodGeoIPFirst,10);
		setCookie('cityHomeEodGeoIPFirst','all',10);
	}
}
function getEodData(eodURL,actionType){
	$.ajax({
	url : eodURL,
	type : "GET",
	success : function(dataHtml){
		var deleteId = 0;
		var showWithoutajax	= 0;
		if($.trim(dataHtml)){
			var ckval 				= $(dataHtml).find('#geo_state').val();
			var ckFlag 				= $(dataHtml).find('#geo_state_1').val();
			var widgetid 			= $(dataHtml).find('#widgetid').val();
			var city_eod_strip_html = $(dataHtml).find('#city_eod_strip').html();
					if(ckFlag==2){
				$("#withoutajax").hide();
				if(actionType==2){					
					$("#bhaskar_eod_new").html(dataHtml);
					//$("#city_eod_strip").remove();
					$('#bhaskar_eod_new').find("#city_eod_strip").remove();
					deleteId = 1;
						
				}else{
					$("#bhaskar_eod_new").html(dataHtml);
					$("#city_eod_strip").remove();	
					$("#bhaskar_eod").prepend("<div id='city_eod_strip' class='cityEodStrip'>"+city_eod_strip_html+"</div>");
				}
				
				$("#bhaskar_eod_new").show();
				if(actionType==1){
					setTimeout(function(){
						if($( "#twoColumn" ).length > 0)
						{
							//$( "#bhaskar_eod_new" ).find("#twoColumn").find("h3").css({"font-size":"20px","line-height":"28px","height":"80px"});
							$( "#bhaskar_eod_new" ).find("#twoColumn").find("h3").css({"font-size":"20px","line-height":"28px"});
						}
						else
						{
							//$( "#bhaskar_eod_new" ).find("h3").css({"font-size":"26px","line-height":"130%","height":"65px"});
							$( "#bhaskar_eod_new" ).find("h3").css({"font-size":"26px","line-height":"130%"});	
						}
					},10);
				}
				
				
			}else{
				jQuery("#withoutajax").show();
				//$("#withoutajax").css({'display':'block'});
				$("#bhaskar_eod_new").hide();
				showWithoutajax = 1;
				//console.log($("#withoutajax").html());
			}
		}else{
			
			var ckval = "all";
			jQuery("#withoutajax").show();
			//jQuery("#withoutajax").css({'display':'block !important'});
			$("#bhaskar_eod_new").hide();
			
		}
		(deleteId ==1)?$("#city_eod_strip").remove():"";
		//(showWithoutajax ==1)?$("#withoutajax").css({'display':'block !important'}):"";
		(showWithoutajax ==1)?jQuery("#withoutajax").show():'';
		if(deleteId ==1 && $("#city_eod_strip").length==0){
			$("#bhaskar_eod").prepend("<div id='city_eod_strip' class='cityEodStrip'>"+city_eod_strip_html+"</div>");	
		}
		setCookie('cityHomeEodGeoIPFirst',ckval,10);
		setCookie('cityHomeEodGeoIPFirstchk',100,10); 
	}
});
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function openVideoPopUp(id)
{
	var fsrc = $("#current_video").attr('src');
	if(fsrc !='' && fsrc!=undefined){
		var ifrmSrc=$('#current_video').attr('src').split("?")[0];
		var newSrc=ifrmSrc+"?autoplayFlag=false&amp;mode=html";
		$("#current_video").attr("src",newSrc);
	}
	openMyModal('/dbtv_video_detail/'+id+'/', 660, 360);return false;
}
jQuery("img.flikrlazy").each(function(){if(jQuery(this).attr('data-original')){jQuery(this).attr('src',jQuery(this).attr('data-original'));jQuery(this).removeAttr('data-original');}});
jQuery('#flicker_dbtv').bxSlider({minSlides: 3,maxSlides: 3, slideMargin: 0,speed :1000,  pager:false,  pagerType:'short', pagerLocation:'bottom',pagerShortSeparator:' of ', autoControls:false, auto:false,infiniteLoop: false, autoHover:true,hideControlOnEnd:true, moveSlides:3});
</script>

<script>
function dispCConverter()
{
	if($("#cc_icon").hasClass('cc-plus'))
	{
		$("#cc_icon").removeClass('cc-plus');
		$("#cc_icon").addClass('cc-minus');
	}else
	{
		$("#cc_icon").removeClass('cc-minus');
		$("#cc_icon").addClass('cc-plus');
	}
	$(".currency-converter-panel-1").slideToggle('slow');
}
</script> </div>

<script>
 $(document).ready( function() {
 $(".content_scroll").mCustomScrollbar({
				scrollButtons:{
				enable:true
			} 
	})	
});

function disp_trends(type)
{
	 if(type == 'trends')
	 {
		 $("#tips").removeClass("active");
		 $("#trends").addClass("active");
		 $("#li_tips").removeClass("active");
		 $("#li_trends").addClass("active");
		 $("#tips_stock_data").hide();
		 $("#trends_stock_data").show();
		 $("#trendsMoreLink").show();
		$("#trends_stock_data").mCustomScrollbar("update");
	 }else if(type == 'tips')
	 {
		$("#trends").removeClass("active");
		$("#tips").addClass("active");
		$("#li_trends").removeClass("active");
		$("#li_tips").addClass("active");
		$("#trends_stock_data").hide(); 
		$("#tips_stock_data").show();
		$("#trendsMoreLink").show();
		$("#tips_stock_data").mCustomScrollbar("update");
	 }
}
</script>
</div>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function cal_url(url)
{
	if(url != '')
	{
		var winObj	=	window.open(url, '_blank');
		if(winObj)
		{
			winObj.focus();
		}
	}
}



 $(document).ready(function(){
   $('#calculator').on('change', function() {  
     var url = this.value;
	if(url != '')
	{    
	 if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Safari') != -1 && navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Chrome') == -1) {
          // window.location.href = url;
		  window.open(url,'','location=yes,width=1300,height=600');
          } else {
                  window.open(url,'_blank');
                  }
	}			  
   });
       
});

</script></div>

//$(document).ready(function () {
	
	var source = comboboxData;
	$("#sub_city_box_mid").autocomplete({
        source: function (request, response) {
			var term = $.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex(request.term)
                , startsWithMatcher = new RegExp("^" + term, "i")
                , startsWith = $.grep(source, function(value) {
                    return startsWithMatcher.test(value.label || value.value || value);
                })
                , containsMatcher = new RegExp(term, "i")
                , contains = $.grep(source, function (value) {
                    return $.inArray(value, startsWith) < 0 && 
                        containsMatcher.test(value.label || value.value || value);
                });
            response(startsWith.concat(contains));
        },
		open: function() {
        $(this).autocomplete("widget")
               .appendTo("#inner_autocomplete")
               .css("position", "static");
    }
    });
	$('#btn3').click(function(){
		$('#sub_city_box_mid').autocomplete('search' , $("#sub_city_box_mid").val());
		$("#sub_city_box_mid").focus();
	});
//});

<script>


function getDataSH(){
	//var shURL 		= 	'/dainikbhaskar2010/religion_selp_help_widget.php';
	var shURL 		= 	'/rashifalSLHPwidge/';
	$.ajax({ 
		type: "GET",
		dataType: "json",
		url: shURL,
		success: function(dataObj) { 
			$(dataObj.data).each(function(key,value){
				//alert("###"+value.image);    
				var sHTML = '<div class="article-list full">';
   				sHTML += '<div class="thumb fl"> <a href="'+value.article+'" title="'+value.title+'"><img src="'+value.image+'" alt="'+value.title+'" title="'+value.title+'" width="85" height="74"></a></div>';
    			sHTML += '<div class="details"> <a href="'+value.article+'" title="'+value.title+'">'+value.title+'</a> </div>'; 
 				sHTML += '</div>';
				$("#shDiv").append(sHTML);  
				
			});
		},
		error: function(error) {
			//alert(error);
		}
	});
}

getDataSH();


</script>

		if (obj.addEventListener){ 
			obj.addEventListener( type, fn, false );
		}else if (obj.attachEvent){ 
			obj["e"+type+fn] = fn; 
			obj[type+fn] = function(){ obj["e"+type+fn]( window.event ); } 
			obj.attachEvent( "on"+type, obj[type+fn] ); 
		}
	}

<script type="text/javascript">

function readCookieRealTime(name) {
	var nameEQ = name + "=";
	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
		if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
	}
	return null;
	}
function createCookieRealTime(name,value,days) {
	if (days) {
		var date = new Date();
		date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
		var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
	}
	else var expires = "";
	var full = window.location.host
    var parts = full.split('.');
    var sub = parts[0];
    var domain = parts[1];
    var type = parts[2];
	if(type=='co'){
		type = type + '.' + parts[3];  	
	}
    var newDomain =  '.'+ domain + '.' + type;
	document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/;domain="+newDomain;
}
var generateUid = function (separator) {
    var delim = separator || "-";
   function S4() {
        return (((1 + Math.random()) * 0x10000) | 0).toString(16).substring(1);
    }
    return (S4() + S4() + delim + S4() + delim + S4() + delim + S4() + delim + S4() + S4() + S4());
};

	bhaskarUID = generateUid();
	createCookieRealTime('bhaskarUID',bhaskarUID,365);
}

<script language='javascript'>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	var Server_URL = 'www.bhaskar.com';
	
	if(Server_URL=='religion.bhaskar.com' || Server_URL=='www.bhaskar.com') {

		var country = read_cookie('Home_300x100'); 
		if(country==null || country=='')
		{	
			var milliseconds = new Date().getTime();	
			$.ajax({
			//url: '/getCountryName/'+milliseconds+'.html',
			url: 'http://realtime.bhaskar.com/get_geo_location.php',
			type: "get",
			dataType: "html",
			success: function( strData ){
				var obj = jQuery.parseJSON( strData);
				country = obj.country_name;
				//alert(country);
				SetCookie('Home_300x100',country,'30');
				callgeoFunction(country);
			}
			}); 
		}
		else 
		{		 
			callgeoFunction(country);
		}
	}
	else{
		var country = 'India'; 
		callgeoFunction(country);
	}
		
function read_cookie(key)
{
    var result;
    return (result = new RegExp('(?:^|; )' + encodeURIComponent(key) + '=([^;]*)').exec(document.cookie)) ? (result[1]) : null;
}

function callgeoFunction(country)
{
	var div = document.getElementsByClassName('geoAd_div');
	for(var i=0; i<div.length; i++)
	{
		getHomePageAds(div[i].id,country);
	}
}

function SetCookie(cookieName,cookieValue,nDays) {
 makeCookie(cookieName,cookieValue,nDays);
 
}
function makeCookie(cookieName,cookieValue,nDays){
	var today = new Date();
 	var expire = new Date();
	 if (nDays==null || nDays==0) nDays=1;
 	expire.setTime(today.getTime() + 3600000*24*nDays);
 	document.cookie = cookieName+"="+escape(cookieValue)+ ";path=/;expires="+expire.toGMTString();
}

function getHomePageAds(id,country)
{
	var milliseconds = new Date().getTime();
	country = country.replace(" ","-");
	$.ajax({
	url: '/getAdAjax/'+id+'/'+country+'.html',
	type: "get",
	dataType: "html",
	success: function( strData ){
		//setTimeout(function(){updateScriptHit(hitId,'ad_hit')},1500);
		$("#"+id).html(strData);
	}
	});
}
});

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
	var c = ca[i];
	while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);	
	if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
}
return null;
}

function createCookie(name,value) {
	var date = new Date();
	var expseconds = 24 * 60 * 60;
	var curseconds = (date.getHours() * 60 * 60) + (date.getMinutes() * 60) + date.getSeconds();
	var midnightseconds = 24 * 60 * 60;
	//var midnightseconds = (date.getHours() * 60 * 60) + ((date.getMinutes() + 3) * 60) + date.getSeconds();
	
	if (curseconds < midnightseconds) {
		expseconds = midnightseconds - parseInt(curseconds);
	}
	
	expseconds = expseconds + (date.getTimezoneOffset() * 60);
	//date.setTime(date.getTime()+(expseconds*1000));
	ndate = new Date((date.getTime()+(expseconds*1000)))	;
	
	var month = new Array();
	month[0] = "Jan";
	month[1] = "Feb";
	month[2] = "Mar";
	month[3] = "Apr";
	month[4] = "May";
	month[5] = "Jun";
	month[6] = "Jul";
	month[7] = "Augt";
	month[8] = "Sep";
	month[9] = "Oct";
	month[10] = "Nov";
	month[11] = "Dec";
	
	var weekday = new Array(7);
	weekday[0]=  "Sun";
	weekday[1] = "Mon";
	weekday[2] = "Tue";
	weekday[3] = "Wed";
	weekday[4] = "Thu";
	weekday[5] = "Fri";
	weekday[6] = "Sat";	
	var expires = "; expires="+weekday[ndate.getDay()]+", "+ndate.getDate()+" " + month[ndate.getMonth()]+ " " + ndate.getFullYear() + " " + ndate.getHours()+":"+ndate.getMinutes()+":59 UTC";
	
	document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
} 
/*function createCookie(name,value,days) {
	if (days) {
		var date = new Date();
		date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
		var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
	}
	else var expires = "";
	document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
}*/
